                 <p itemprop="description" lang="en">
                  Very good pho and lemon grass chicken. Next table had the crab curry and it looked delicious. I have known the owner Tam from previous business about 12 years ago and church and he was/is a classy guy. Service is good too, water was often re-filled. Hate it when there's no water.

                  <span class="rating-qualifier">
                   <meta content="2015-04-03" itemprop="datePublished"/>
                   4/3/2015
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <p itemprop="description" lang="en">
                  Love this place!
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  Parking is a little hard though. Private lot, but very tight and very limited. Street parking is also limited. So far, I've been very lucky with parking.
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  Service is fast and workers are always friendly. Very welcoming environment.

               <div class="review-wrapper">
                <div class="review-content">
                 <div class="biz-rating biz-rating-very-large clearfix">
                  <div itemprop="reviewRating" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating">
                   <div class="rating-very-large">
                    <i class="star-img stars_3" title="3.0 star rating">
                     <img alt="3.0 star rating" class="offscreen" height="303" src="//s3-media4.fl.yelpcdn.com/assets/srv0/yelp_styleguide/c2252a4cd43e/assets/img/stars/stars_map.png" width="84"/>
                    </i>
                    <meta content="3.0" itemprop="ratingValue"/>
                   </div>
                  </div>
                  <span class="rating-qualifier">
                   <meta content="2015-03-22" itemprop="datePublished"/>
                   3/22/2015
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <div class="review_tags">
                  <span class="i-wrap ig-wrap-common i-18x18_duke_c-common-wrap review-tag">
                   <i class="i ig-common i-18x18_duke_c-common">
                   </i>
                   7 check-ins
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <p itemprop="description" lang="en">
                  Bac Nam is a casual restaurant that's good for dinning in and take out. We've called ahead and had lunch for 20 in their second dinning room, food came out in a reasonable amount of time, and everyone generally enjoyed their meal.
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  While I've tried different items like their Green Papaya Salad, Pork Chops, Spring Rolls, Vermicelli Noodles and Fried Shrimp, my hands down favorite is the Crab Curry with French Bread. This is easy luxury. No shells, no fuss. The curry is thick and rich with lots of real crab. Skip the rice and scoop up the curry with hunks of crusty bread. If you like curry and crab, try this!
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  When you check out Bac Nam here's what you need to know. They have a small parking lot or find street parking. They have individual plates and dishes meant to be eaten family style, like, did I mention, this Crab Curry they make? Haha
                 </p>

                 <p itemprop="description" lang="en">
                  Came here with the work crew and had the Pho sadly the noodles were overcooked otherwise it was ok, went again and this time stayed away from the Pho and was really happy with the beef curry although it came in a shallow bowl actually a plate it was very flavorful and tasty I think I found my favorite here...
                  <br/>
                  The service seemed pretty quick and water was refilled often so no complaints there, we walked so didn't have to deal with looking for parking although I'm not sure as I don't think there is that much parking around. But I'm sure I'll be back again.
                 </p>

               <div class="review-wrapper">
                <div class="review-content">
                 <div class="biz-rating biz-rating-very-large clearfix">
                  <div itemprop="reviewRating" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating">
                   <div class="rating-very-large">
                    <i class="star-img stars_4" title="4.0 star rating">
                     <img alt="4.0 star rating" class="offscreen" height="303" src="//s3-media4.fl.yelpcdn.com/assets/srv0/yelp_styleguide/c2252a4cd43e/assets/img/stars/stars_map.png" width="84"/>
                    </i>
                    <meta content="4.0" itemprop="ratingValue"/>
                   </div>
                  </div>
                  <span class="rating-qualifier">
                   <meta content="2014-09-03" itemprop="datePublished"/>
                   9/3/2014
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <div class="review_tags">
                  <span class="i-wrap ig-wrap-common i-18x18_checkin_c-common-wrap review-tag">
                   <i class="i ig-common i-18x18_checkin_c-common">
                   </i>
                   4 check-ins
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <p itemprop="description" lang="en">
                  What a great find after living my entire life as a townie and only now patronizing this establishment.
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  I have to apologize that I was so hungry that I just threw everything in and took a messy (still delicious) picture.
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  I ordered the rare steak pho and it was soooooo goood! The broth was savory, but not overpowering. Most Pho places have lighter broths, and if it is savory it tends to be oily or too salty for my taste.
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  The noodles were cooked perfectly and they didn't swell up while I was eating; it didn't feel like that bottomless bowl of noodles with cloudy
                  <br/>
                  Broth that you might sometimes get at other restaurants.
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  The beef was sliced a bit on the thicker side, and I prefer thinner slices.
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  My friend had the spring roll salad and he jumped into it so quicky that I didn't have time to take a picture. I guess I could have because it would still look yummy!
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  The service was fast and efficient. Its a nice cool place and seats more than it appears from the outside. Even during the lunch hour rush we were served promptly and politely.I did feel a bit rushed at times. I guess they're used to people being in a rush, and faster quality service is better than slow poor service anyday.
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  They do take out, so call ahead and there's parking on the street or in the back of the building.
                 </p>

               <div class="review-wrapper">
                <div class="review-content">
                 <div class="biz-rating biz-rating-very-large clearfix">
                  <div itemprop="reviewRating" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating">
                   <div class="rating-very-large">
                    <i class="star-img stars_5" title="5.0 star rating">
                     <img alt="5.0 star rating" class="offscreen" height="303" src="//s3-media4.fl.yelpcdn.com/assets/srv0/yelp_styleguide/c2252a4cd43e/assets/img/stars/stars_map.png" width="84"/>
                    </i>
                    <meta content="5.0" itemprop="ratingValue"/>
                   </div>
                  </div>
                  <span class="rating-qualifier">
                   <meta content="2014-06-16" itemprop="datePublished"/>
                   6/16/2014
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <div class="review_tags">
                  <span class="i-wrap ig-wrap-common i-18x18_checkin_c-common-wrap review-tag">
                   <i class="i ig-common i-18x18_checkin_c-common">
                   </i>
                   3 check-ins
                  </span>
                  <div class="review-favorites-lists">
                   <span class="i-wrap ig-wrap-common i-tag-menu-common-wrap review-tag">
                    <i class="i ig-common i-tag-menu-common">
                    </i>
                    Listed in
                    <a href="/list/go-beyond-the-pho-honolulu" title="What the pho to order?">
                     Go beyond the pho!
                    </a>
                   </span>
                  </div>
                 </div>
                 <p itemprop="description" lang="en">
                  For those of you who have not crossed over or beyond the "pho" line, there is another world of culinary bliss waiting to tantalize your palate in Vietnamese cuisine.
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  I have been a patron of Bac Nam forever or rather for last 10 years when they first opened in the early summer of 2004. I recalled how it was just a tiny place, about half the size of its current space. The entire restaurant used to be only the size of its current ewa-end section but they've since doubled in size due to their authentic and amazing food. In their early days, it was so cute and adorable to see their 2 kids (maybe they didn't think so at the time) frequently help out at the restaurant. The kids measured hip-high and they gave good service like setting up the eating utensils, carried glasses of water to the tables for the customers and even gave us the final check to pay. The value of work ethics were taught very early on to these kids. Now they're all teenagers and they still help out around the restaurant.
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  From the get go, the food was amazing and it is still as awesome as it were in those days. As with any restaurants, there is no perfect restaurant serving all perfect dishes. You just have to know what items to order and this holds true for any restaurants or eateries. Bac Nam's food is fantastic and they have such a loyal fan base and repeat customers keep on spreading the word. I love 80% of their menu items and my "favs" are always come out consistently great. Someone can blindfold me and have me order in this manner and I still wouldn't mind eating whatever dish my finger happened to select at that particular moment. I never get tired of eating there so I go often. The added bonus Bac Nam has is that they allow BYOB; it's just a great value and service they provide. Such an awesome and hardworking family but still friendly and humble.
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  Bac Nam is my to go place whenever I want to eat really good and flavorful. I'm not a bland-foodie fan. There are some dishes requiring lots of work and time and Bac Nam do them so well instead of putting out a simple menu commonly seen here in many Vietnamese restaurants. Amazing cook the lady owner is; she used to be the cook at Pho One before they struck out on their own. I wish I could cook like her; especially her incredible nuoc mam sauce. After many attempts to re-create this Vietnamese fish sauce, I gave up on trying.
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  Throughout the years, I've introduced many friends, work associates and visitors from all over to Bac Nam and 99 percent of them have requested to eat at Bac Nam when they've returned to the island. One down side I sometimes wish they could change: use round tables but it would be impractical with their current space's configuration. Now wouldn't that make it an even better family-style restaurant?
                 </p>

               <div class="review-wrapper">
                <div class="review-content">
                 <div class="biz-rating biz-rating-very-large clearfix">
                  <div itemprop="reviewRating" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating">
                   <div class="rating-very-large">
                    <i class="star-img stars_2" title="2.0 star rating">
                     <img alt="2.0 star rating" class="offscreen" height="303" src="//s3-media4.fl.yelpcdn.com/assets/srv0/yelp_styleguide/c2252a4cd43e/assets/img/stars/stars_map.png" width="84"/>
                    </i>
                    <meta content="2.0" itemprop="ratingValue"/>
                   </div>
                  </div>
                  <span class="rating-qualifier">
                   <meta content="2014-05-02" itemprop="datePublished"/>
                   5/2/2014
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <div class="review_tags">
                  <span class="i-wrap ig-wrap-common i-18x18_checkin_c-common-wrap review-tag">
                   <i class="i ig-common i-18x18_checkin_c-common">
                   </i>
                   1 check-in
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <p itemprop="description" lang="en">
                  It has been many years since I last ate here. The last time I came here was to celebrate a friend's 60th birthday where we took the whole side dining room and the front tables were used as a buffet table. There were only a few tables available for walk-in so this place was packed. Because the menu was pre-ordered, food came out and it was a great experience.
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  I came here last night with 6 other people and walked out soooooo disappointed. It was so awful I don't even know where to start.
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  First of all, the food that came out was barely warm. Granted I had a meeting at nearby Zippy's so I came in a little late but as I sat down and several dishes came out of the kitchen and took some food, it was barely warm!
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  Next, between the 7 of us we ordered 6 dishes (french bread and rice NOT included in the 6), our server FORGOT 2 of them! Our server was perhaps the son of the owner and probably a student and he may have tried hard but didn't deliver the minimum service that we deserve.
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  I had to ask for water refills THREE times before he brought over the pitcher. Keep in mind that the third time I ended up being sarcastic to his father who probably put some heat on the son who then immediately came over. By the time he filled all cups, I was the last one and my cup didn't even make it halfway full. Did he bother to come back with more water? NO!!!
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  We asked for more rice as the crab curry dish came out and waited for about 10 mins and nothing was brought over. I then walked up and asked the father about our rice order and then the son comes over with a plate of rice with some green onions on top. But the rice was COLD!!!
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  Being fluent in Japanese there were quite a few tables with Japanese tourists dining so this place was PACKED. If you're going to be featured in a guidebook you need to have proper servers and this young boy should be a busboy handling water, cleaning tables, etc. but NOT as a waiter. Perhaps this place cannot facilitate a full house and we just happened to dine on a bad day? I don't know...
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  Here is what we ate:
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  1) Deep-Fried Stuffed Chicken Wings (3/5)
                  <br/>
                  By the time I arrived it was sitting on the table and everyone already had their share so naturally it was cold. Would have tasted better but it was generously stuffed with meat and some veggies and came with the traditional NUOC CHAM sauce (fish sauce, sugar, lemon, shredded carrots, chili and sugar).
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  2) Grilled beef rolls w/ fresh veggies wrapped in rice paper (2/5) in Vietnamese BA LA LOT (?)
                  <br/>
                  This dish was also on the table when I arrived so it was also cold. You had to wrap them up as it was served nicely on a platter. I was fortunate to have them rolled by a friend as I didn't want to struggle and get my hands dirty! The meat was flavorful but a little on the dry side. You dip them in the NUOC CHAM sauce so it was juicy but I first tried it "as-is" where I found out it needed some moisture.
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  3) Crab Curry (3/5)
                  <br/>
                  A very flavorful dish and it was also barely warm when it arrived on our table. I noticed neighboring tables with Japanese nationals had this same dish so I had my hopes high. It was too gloppy with too much cornstarch to thicken it. This dish here may be convenient as only the crab meat is served but the curry crab at Mai Lan on Keeaumoku which uses a whole dungeness crab with shell is much tastier in my opinion. This was served with both a toasted french bread roll (the only thing that came out of the kitchen that night for me) and a plate of rice.
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  4) Tamarind Shrimp (4/5)
                  <br/>
                  Also very flavorful and you can taste the tamarind sauce. I found myself wanting more sauce to spoon over my rice! The shell was soft so you could eat the whole thing. Again, the shrimp came out warm where it would have been better piping HOT.
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  5) Lamb Curry (2/5)
                  <br/>
                  This is one of the dishes our server forgot to put in the order. When it came out it was barely warm!!! The meat was tender and the sauce was good but again, gloppy sauce.
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  I feel bad writing this review. Food was overall disappointing with AWFUL service. It'll be a looooong time if I decide to come back here to dine again.
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  NOTES:
                  <br/>
                  1) Parking available behind the restaurant specifically for Bac Nam (signs available for the stalls).
                  <br/>
                  2) Despite the bad service our leader opted to give 20% tip.
                  <br/>
                  3) Our server forgot our order of BUN XIAO (mung bean crepe) and we cancelled it.
                  <br/>
                  4) BYOB here with no corkage fee.
                 </p>

                   <meta content="2014-10-02" itemprop="datePublished"/>
                   10/2/2014
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <div class="review_tags">
                  <span class="i-wrap ig-wrap-common i-18x18_checkin_c-common-wrap review-tag">
                   <i class="i ig-common i-18x18_checkin_c-common">
                   </i>
                   1 check-in
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <p itemprop="description" lang="en">
                  What a great restaurant!
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  My wife and I were fortunate to meet Lien V. at one of the Kbay events a couple of weeks ago. New friends we met that evening said we should ask Lien where to get good Vietnamese food. Not only did she have a bunch of recommendations, she invited us to dinner!
                  <br/>
                  We met her at Bac Nam and were greeted warmly at the restaurant. Lien and went over the menu with us and gave us an idea of what to order. We settled on lamb curry, tamarind shrimp, and the vietnamese crepe.
                  <br/>
                  Everything was so good! The crepe was light and crispy on the outside, and filled with hearty goodness on the inside. The lamb curry was so flavorful and delicious. It was unlike anything I have had before....not gamey, but tender and yummy. The tamarind shrimp was the table favorite. A little pungent, this dish was sweet, sour, and savory at the same time. It was very bright and fresh tasting....truly an amazing dish...we will sooo be back. If you go for one dish here...that would be it!
                  <br/>
                  We cant wait for our next dinner with Lien!
                 </p>

               <div class="review-wrapper">
                <div class="review-content">
                 <div class="biz-rating biz-rating-very-large clearfix">
                  <div itemprop="reviewRating" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating">
                   <div class="rating-very-large">
                    <i class="star-img stars_4" title="4.0 star rating">
                     <img alt="4.0 star rating" class="offscreen" height="303" src="//s3-media4.fl.yelpcdn.com/assets/srv0/yelp_styleguide/c2252a4cd43e/assets/img/stars/stars_map.png" width="84"/>
                    </i>
                    <meta content="4.0" itemprop="ratingValue"/>
                   </div>
                  </div>
                  <span class="rating-qualifier">
                   <meta content="2014-03-19" itemprop="datePublished"/>
                   3/19/2014
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <div class="review_tags">
                  <span class="i-wrap ig-wrap-common i-18x18_checkin_c-common-wrap review-tag">
                   <i class="i ig-common i-18x18_checkin_c-common">
                   </i>
                   1 check-in
                  </span>
                  <div class="review-favorites-lists">
                   <span class="i-wrap ig-wrap-common i-tag-menu-common-wrap review-tag">
                    <i class="i ig-common i-tag-menu-common">
                    </i>
                    Listed in
                    <a href="/list/asian-invasion-honolulu-2" title="where the asians go to criticize non-asians">
                     Asian Invasion
                    </a>
                    ,
                    <a href="/list/fetch-my-stretchy-pants-quick-honolulu" title="places that conquer my stomach capacity">
                     Fetch my Stretchy Pants Quick!
                    </a>
                    ,
                    <a href="/list/ramen-and-saimin-and-pho-honolulu" title="yes, they're different, and no, this is not your average college eats.....">
                     RAMEN and SAIMIN and PHO
                    </a>
                   </span>
                  </div>
                 </div>
                 <p itemprop="description" lang="en">
                  PHO PHO PHO!
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  i should mention.... i didn't have the pho here :P
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  i DID have the ox tail.... OX TAIL OX TAIL OX TAIL!
                  <a href="http://www.yelp.com/biz_photos/bac-nam-honolulu?userid=DfT00CYynx9wX4qG4f5hPA#P-gb29Y8wbK-5mVoQcEfqw">
                   yelp.com/biz_photos/bac-
                  </a>
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  which by the way, is pretty delicious. plenty plenty pieces of ox tail. meaty, hot, and delicious. served with a lot of ginger, and rice on the side.... what more could you want?
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  i know what more you could want..... crispy spring rolls. crispy-fried and slightly flaky on the outside with your standard lettuce leaf, noodles, cucumber and mint.... both refreshing and savory. you gotta get this too with your pho... or ox tail.... or whatever you decide to try here.
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  the space is much larger than i thought, and deceiving from the outside.
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  service is ok. not 5 star service, but our orders came out right, and my questions were answered.
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  the extremely bad part about this restaurant is parking. there is a very small lot in the back area that is hard to navigate, and has very few stalls. of course, there is always street parking...... but only if it is available :/
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  i'll be back b/c well... its close to where i live, and the food is decent :) i spotted some yelper on here talking about "Vietnamese kalbi" and that is definitely something i'm going to try on another visit!
                 </p>

                   <div class="photo-box photo-box--interactive">

                    <div class="photo-box-overlay js-overlay">
                     <div class="photo-box-overlay_caption">
                      Ox tail soup w/rice

                 <p itemprop="description" lang="en">
                  Pretty good chicken curry. Chicken is served with bones &amp; skin on as the waiter told me was Vietnamese style. Good flavor. Side of rice had bits of chopped garlic which was a nice touch. Small location off of King Street. Perfect for a quick lunch.
                 </p>

                 <div class="biz-rating biz-rating-very-large clearfix">
                  <div itemprop="reviewRating" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating">
                   <div class="rating-very-large">
                    <i class="star-img stars_4" title="4.0 star rating">
                     <img alt="4.0 star rating" class="offscreen" height="303" src="//s3-media4.fl.yelpcdn.com/assets/srv0/yelp_styleguide/c2252a4cd43e/assets/img/stars/stars_map.png" width="84"/>
                    </i>
                    <meta content="4.0" itemprop="ratingValue"/>
                   </div>
                  </div>
                  <span class="rating-qualifier">
                   <meta content="2014-01-08" itemprop="datePublished"/>
                   1/8/2014
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <div class="review_tags">
                  <span class="i-wrap ig-wrap-common i-18x18_checkin_c-common-wrap review-tag">
                   <i class="i ig-common i-18x18_checkin_c-common">
                   </i>
                   5 check-ins
                  </span>
                  <div class="review-favorites-lists">
                   <span class="i-wrap ig-wrap-common i-tag-menu-common-wrap review-tag">
                    <i class="i ig-common i-tag-menu-common">
                    </i>
                    Listed in
                    <a href="/list/hungry-but-healthy-honolulu" title="Feeding your body in more ways then one, keeping it fresh and light!">
                     Hungry but healthy
                    </a>
                   </span>
                  </div>
                 </div>
                 <p itemprop="description" lang="en">
                  Pho...I've had a love/hate relationship with you for years....but luckily because of places like Bac Nam...it's all about the love now. Originally the hate came from the presence of cilantro and ignorance about seasoning the broth with sauces.
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  Bac nam is frequently crowded but once you get a seat, the wait help is very efficient. I love the beef pho (no cilantro!) And the spring rolls. I wish the spring rolls came with additional veggies with the lettuce wraps. The pho broth itself is great and the portions big enough for at least two meals. I want to try ox tail and summer rolls on my next visit but I love pho so much I don't know if I'll be able to be adventurous.
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  The weather has been cold lately, I think it's time to go back for some pho.
                 </p>

                  <div itemprop="reviewRating" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating">
                   <div class="rating-very-large">
                    <i class="star-img stars_5" title="5.0 star rating">
                     <img alt="5.0 star rating" class="offscreen" height="303" src="//s3-media4.fl.yelpcdn.com/assets/srv0/yelp_styleguide/c2252a4cd43e/assets/img/stars/stars_map.png" width="84"/>

                 <div class="review_tags">
                  <span class="i-wrap ig-wrap-common i-18x18_checkin_c-common-wrap review-tag">

                   </i>
                   1 check-in
                  </span>

                 <p itemprop="description" lang="en">
                  You want some pretty legit Pho this is the place to go to. I'm going straight to the food in this review because I have yet to find another place that would make pho with the broth being clean but not light. The broth had such an explosion of flavors that I've never had at other places that served Pho. I also tried their spring rolls with vermecilli which was pretty awesome too. But their star entree is Pho.
                  <br/>
                  Parking is a hassle I have to say. Scored with a stall right in front of the restaurant but others might not be as lucky.  Looks like it's just street parking. Also located near the intersection of King St and Pensacola St..
                 </p>

               <div class="review-wrapper">
                <div class="review-content">
                 <div class="biz-rating biz-rating-very-large clearfix">
                  <div itemprop="reviewRating" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating">
                   <div class="rating-very-large">
                    <i class="star-img stars_4" title="4.0 star rating">
                     <img alt="4.0 star rating" class="offscreen" height="303" src="//s3-media4.fl.yelpcdn.com/assets/srv0/yelp_styleguide/c2252a4cd43e/assets/img/stars/stars_map.png" width="84"/>
                    </i>
                    <meta content="4.0" itemprop="ratingValue"/>
                   </div>
                  </div>
                  <span class="rating-qualifier">
                   <meta content="2014-05-02" itemprop="datePublished"/>
                   5/2/2014
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <div class="review_tags">
                  <div class="review-favorites-lists">
                   <span class="i-wrap ig-wrap-common i-tag-menu-common-wrap review-tag">
                    <i class="i ig-common i-tag-menu-common">
                    </i>
                    Listed in
                    <a href="/list/top-5-pho-places-on-oahu-honolulu" title="No entry level spots, just pure hardcore pho.">
                     Top 5 Pho Places on Oahu
                    </a>
                   </span>
                  </div>
                 </div>
                 <p itemprop="description" lang="en">
                  Very seldom do I ever go to a pho/Vietnamese restaurant and not order pho. If I really have to though, Bac Nam is the place I would go.
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  The pho here isn't terrible, but quite average. Multiple times I've been here and the pho was consistent, but there isn't much flavor in their broth. Again, this isn't where you want to go for pho. You're going to have to be much more adventurous, you know, order the dishes that you have a hard time pronouncing.
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  The bun rieu cua(crab noodle soup) is excellent. I wouldn't know if it was truly authentic or not but in many ways, it is enjoyable. Even putting the soup with some rice is tasty.
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  Ca ri bo (Vietnamese beef curry) is another favorite of mine here. For those who don't like beef curry, try the chicken curry(ca ri ga). It is milder than Indian or Thai curry but retains the thickness via coconut milk.
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  Service here is usually pretty good. Mom and pop joint. Parking is difficult. They do have parking in the rear, but for this area, I normally enjoy parking in the streets more.
                 </p>
                </div>

                  <div class="review-favorites-lists">
                   <span class="i-wrap ig-wrap-common i-tag-menu-common-wrap review-tag">
                    <i class="i ig-common i-tag-menu-common">
                    </i>
                    Listed in
                    <a href="/list/pho-sho-honolulu" title="Vietnamese please">
                     Pho Sho'
                    </a>
                   </span>
                  </div>
                 </div>
                 <p itemprop="description" lang="en">
                  Not a bad pho place. I had a small tendon pho for about $7. The broth was ok, a little too heavy on the anise for me. A quirky thing is that if you want two choices of topping, you must get a large for about $10. But then the combo pho is about $10 and includes like 6 toppings. Go figure.
                 </p>

                 <span class="js-expandable-comment comment-truncated">
                  <span class="js-content-toggleable">
                   Decent option for Vietnamese. I had the grilled pork chop rice which was pretty good, two big
                  </span>
                  <span class="js-content-toggleable hidden">
                   Decent option for Vietnamese. I had the grilled pork chop rice which was pretty good, two big chops, grilled nicely Vietnamese style. I would recommend this. My husband had the BBQ pork and shrimp which was good as well. I did detect that the dishes had a lot of MSG, though. I'd come back for the pho if I was in the 'hood. Service was nice and attentive.
                  </span>

                 <p itemprop="description" lang="en">

                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  Food was great, the restaurant itself is a little weird. It was super bright in there, like ridiculously bright I felt like I was in an office. The seating was also a little funky.

               <div class="review-wrapper">
                <div class="review-content">
                 <div class="biz-rating biz-rating-very-large clearfix">
                  <div itemprop="reviewRating" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating">
                   <div class="rating-very-large">
                    <i class="star-img stars_2" title="2.0 star rating">
                     <img alt="2.0 star rating" class="offscreen" height="303" src="//s3-media4.fl.yelpcdn.com/assets/srv0/yelp_styleguide/c2252a4cd43e/assets/img/stars/stars_map.png" width="84"/>
                    </i>
                    <meta content="2.0" itemprop="ratingValue"/>
                   </div>
                  </div>
                  <span class="rating-qualifier">
                   <meta content="2015-04-29" itemprop="datePublished"/>
                   4/29/2015
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <p itemprop="description" lang="en">
                  Looking at the good reviews and compliments over the crab curry, we decided to have a dinner at this restaurant.
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  As many people have mentioned, the parking is very limited, but we luckily found a street parking right in front of the restaurant.
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  Once we entered the restaurant, the waiter immediately brought the bilingual menu mainly in Japanese with small English descriptions. While me and my parents are Japanese, my husband and his family are not. My husband side was pretty confused, I could see there are some descriptions lacking in details in English and I translated it for them. The waiter seemed like they don't care, and very unfriendly when I asked some questions about menu or asked for extra bowls to share the dishes.
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  The pho was ok, and the crab curry was ok. Crab curry was very mild flavor, no spiciness, lots of crabmeat (tasted like canned crabmeat tho), I could feel small pieces of shell in the curry..
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  With the price, food was ok, and the service was not comfortable, it was rather disappointing experience.
                 </p>
                </div>

               <div class="review-wrapper">
                <div class="review-content">
                 <div class="biz-rating biz-rating-very-large clearfix">
                  <div itemprop="reviewRating" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating">
                   <div class="rating-very-large">
                    <i class="star-img stars_4" title="4.0 star rating">
                     <img alt="4.0 star rating" class="offscreen" height="303" src="//s3-media4.fl.yelpcdn.com/assets/srv0/yelp_styleguide/c2252a4cd43e/assets/img/stars/stars_map.png" width="84"/>
                    </i>
                    <meta content="4.0" itemprop="ratingValue"/>
                   </div>
                  </div>
                  <span class="rating-qualifier">
                   <meta content="2014-11-20" itemprop="datePublished"/>
                   11/20/2014
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <div class="review_tags">
                  <span class="i-wrap ig-wrap-common i-18x18_checkin_c-common-wrap review-tag">
                   <i class="i ig-common i-18x18_checkin_c-common">
                   </i>
                   1 check-in
                  </span>
                  <div class="review-favorites-lists">
                   <span class="i-wrap ig-wrap-common i-tag-menu-common-wrap review-tag">
                    <i class="i ig-common i-tag-menu-common">
                    </i>
                    Listed in
                    <a href="/list/paolas-yelp-100-review-challenge-2014-honolulu" title="Check out my 100 (hopefully more!) reviews of 2014 as I explore my new home, Honolulu">
                     Paola's Yelp 100 Review Challenge 2014
                    </a>
                   </span>
                  </div>
                 </div>
                 <p itemprop="description" lang="en">
                  This place is great, and I'm stoked that it's only a block away from my office. I went here on the hottest day of the year, so I wasn't going to get my usual bowl of pho. I decided to try their thit bo nuong la lot (beef wrapped in betel leaves). It comes with rice paper and a bowl of hot water that you use to soften the paper to wrap around the wrapped beef. And it comes with lettuce leaves in case you want to wrap all of that in lettuce, as well as a small side of rice noodles. It was so, so tasty and I would highly recommend it if you want something else other than pho.
                 </p>
                </div>

                 <div class="biz-rating biz-rating-very-large clearfix">
                  <div itemprop="reviewRating" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating">
                   <div class="rating-very-large">
                    <i class="star-img stars_5" title="5.0 star rating">
                     <img alt="5.0 star rating" class="offscreen" height="303" src="//s3-media4.fl.yelpcdn.com/assets/srv0/yelp_styleguide/c2252a4cd43e/assets/img/stars/stars_map.png" width="84"/>
                    </i>
                    <meta content="5.0" itemprop="ratingValue"/>
                   </div>

                  <span class="rating-qualifier">
                   <meta content="2014-11-21" itemprop="datePublished"/>
                   11/21/2014
                  </span>

                 <p itemprop="description" lang="en">
                  I'm not a huge fan of vietnamese food like pho but this place is really good! The service was slow when the older man (I think the owner?) was the waiter, but the young waiter is very friendly and quick :)
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  I love the spring rolls. Its perfectly crispy and I like the crab pho noodle. You could tell they use real crab because I expected imitation crab. It adds a sweet taste to the broth. What they are known for is their crab meat curry which is really good too. It's probably the priciest thing on their menu but it is worth trying. I got it with rice but I think I'll try it with french bread next time. All the food seems really good so I want to try other things next time.
                 </p>
                </div>

               <div class="review-wrapper">
                <div class="review-content">
                 <div class="biz-rating biz-rating-very-large clearfix">
                  <div itemprop="reviewRating" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating">
                   <div class="rating-very-large">
                    <i class="star-img stars_4" title="4.0 star rating">
                     <img alt="4.0 star rating" class="offscreen" height="303" src="//s3-media4.fl.yelpcdn.com/assets/srv0/yelp_styleguide/c2252a4cd43e/assets/img/stars/stars_map.png" width="84"/>
                    </i>
                    <meta content="4.0" itemprop="ratingValue"/>
                   </div>
                  </div>
                  <span class="rating-qualifier">
                   <meta content="2013-09-17" itemprop="datePublished"/>
                   9/17/2013
                   <small class="bullet-before has-archived-review">
                    <strong class="i-wrap ig-wrap-common i-updated-review-common-wrap">
                     <i class="i ig-common i-updated-review-common">
                     </i>
                     Updated review
                    </strong>
                   </small>
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <p itemprop="description" lang="en">
                  I still love Bac Nam. The owner remembers me from my frequent visits and was attentive and always friendly. For lunch I had the POUNDED SHRIMP BUN and my handsome lunch date had the PRAWN CURRY with rice. He loved the curry, and the prawns were real prawns (nice sized) but the skin was on it so he has to peel them off. Minus points for that but I get it that the skin makes the dish taste oh-so-tons better. I also had an order of the SHRIMP SUMMER ROLL which was fresh and delicate.
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  I love that there's a small parking lot in the back just after the restaurant and some metered parking out front.
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  I've come here often before for dinner. It's BYOB which is always a plus. A lot of locals roll up in here, as well as tourists especially Japanese nationals. They know what's up! Can't wait to eat here again and maybe have some pho next time.
                 </p>

                   <i class="star-img stars_5" title="5.0 star rating">
                    <img alt="5.0 star rating" class="offscreen" height="303" src="//s3-media4.fl.yelpcdn.com/assets/srv0/yelp_styleguide/c2252a4cd43e/assets/img/stars/stars_map.png" width="84"/>

                 <span class="js-expandable-comment comment-truncated">
                  <span class="js-content-toggleable">
                   I heart Bac Nam! Thought I wrote a review a while back but I guess not. The owner is great, very
                  </span>
                  <span class="js-content-toggleable hidden">
                   I heart Bac Nam! Thought I wrote a review a while back but I guess not. The owner is great, very personable and is there for you as a customer.
                   <br/>
                   <br/>
                   - Shaken Beef: tender beef chunks on a flavorful bed of lettuce, cucumber, and other veggies. Delightful sauce, yum. Prices went up though, used to be $11 months ago, now it's $13. I normally order it with rice on the side. I never eat the entire thing in one sitting, so I take a small box home. It's worth it.
                   <br/>
                   - Lamb Curry: heavenly goodness! ask for rice on the side. you will love it, so balanced. Tender pieces of lamb, with carrots, potatoes. I'm smiling just thinking about it.
                   <br/>
                   - Chicken Curry Noodles: my new favorite dish for only $8.95! I used to always get the shaken beef but this dish on the menu caught my eye recently. I was absolutely thrilled when I ate it, devoured what I could and brought the rest home...I thoroughly enjoyed it at the second seating. Dark chicken meat, cut carefully from a whole chicken, with thin vermicelli noodles, carrots, potatoes, onions. Fresh mint and bean sprouts thrown in. DELICIOUS AND HAPPY TUMMY.
                   <br/>
                   - Spring Rolls: now we're talking. Home made, wonderful fried pillows of flavor-balanced meat, veggies.
                   <br/>
                   - Summer Rolls: equally wonderful, soft pillows. Sauce is good.
                   <br/>
                   - Dumplings: flavorful but the wrapper is quite thick so you have to eat it in tiny bites or you could choke on it. really.
                   <br/>
                   <br/>
                   The decor is simple, seems to be popular with the Japanese nationals and tourists. There's street parking after 6:30pm on King St, and a small back parking lot with a few spaces. The place started out tiny with just maybe 7 small tables, you'd have to walk thru the kitchen to get to the back restroom. Last year they expanded with a back room, at least 5 more tables and full access to the restroom. :-) You will love!
                  </span>

                  </a>

                 <div class="biz-rating biz-rating-very-large clearfix">
                  <div itemprop="reviewRating" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating">
                   <div class="rating-very-large">
                    <i class="star-img stars_3" title="3.0 star rating">
                     <img alt="3.0 star rating" class="offscreen" height="303" src="//s3-media4.fl.yelpcdn.com/assets/srv0/yelp_styleguide/c2252a4cd43e/assets/img/stars/stars_map.png" width="84"/>
                    </i>
                    <meta content="3.0" itemprop="ratingValue"/>
                   </div>
                  </div>
                  <span class="rating-qualifier">
                   <meta content="2014-03-18" itemprop="datePublished"/>
                   3/18/2014
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <div class="review_tags">
                  <span class="i-wrap ig-wrap-common i-18x18_checkin_c-common-wrap review-tag">
                   <i class="i ig-common i-18x18_checkin_c-common">
                   </i>
                   2 check-ins
                  </span>
                  <div class="review-favorites-lists">
                   <span class="i-wrap ig-wrap-common i-tag-menu-common-wrap review-tag">
                    <i class="i ig-common i-tag-menu-common">
                    </i>
                    Listed in
                    <a href="/list/pho-far-and-wide-honolulu" title="The eternal hangover fix and vietnamese comfort food">
                     Pho far and wide!
                    </a>
                   </span>
                  </div>
                 </div>
                 <p itemprop="description" lang="en">
                  Bac Nam is located near the intersection of Pensacola and King. It's open for lunch from 10:30am UNTIL 2:30pm and reopens at 5:00pm until 9:00pm for dinner. I'd say try not to come right at 2:30pm because they close promptly at 2:30 and sometimes a few minutes before.
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  Pros: always great, friendly, and prompt service; tasty pho
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  Cons: always feel like MSG overload post-meal; not many pho options; sometimes the staff can disappear into the kitchen for extended periods of time
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  Pho is available either as beef, chicken, seafood, or combination in small or large sizes. If you like just rare beef and tendon like me, you're out of luck. Also, don't worry if you don't see sate at the table (the spicy sauce in oil)...you just have to request it!
                 </p>

                <div class="review-content">
                 <div class="biz-rating biz-rating-very-large clearfix">
                  <div itemprop="reviewRating" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating">
                   <div class="rating-very-large">
                    <i class="star-img stars_5" title="5.0 star rating">
                     <img alt="5.0 star rating" class="offscreen" height="303" src="//s3-media4.fl.yelpcdn.com/assets/srv0/yelp_styleguide/c2252a4cd43e/assets/img/stars/stars_map.png" width="84"/>
                    </i>
                    <meta content="5.0" itemprop="ratingValue"/>
                   </div>

                  <span class="rating-qualifier">
                   <meta content="2014-03-10" itemprop="datePublished"/>
                   3/10/2014
                  </span>

                 <p itemprop="description" lang="en">
                  Oh my gosh, how have I never been here before?! This place has sweet pho.. But what you need to come here for is the grilled beef wrapped in lot leaf! Tender beef is grilled in a lot lead, you're given rice paper wraps (and hot water) to soften the rice paper, and then you wrap the beef with your fillings (rice noodles, cucumbers, veggie mix, peanuts, mint leaves, lettuce) and dip it in a sweet sauce. Oh dear lord, I'm never going back to spring rolls again! Go here and try this now, these steak things are amaaaazing!!!
                 </p>

               <div class="review-wrapper">
                <div class="review-content">
                 <div class="biz-rating biz-rating-very-large clearfix">
                  <div itemprop="reviewRating" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating">
                   <div class="rating-very-large">
                    <i class="star-img stars_4" title="4.0 star rating">
                     <img alt="4.0 star rating" class="offscreen" height="303" src="//s3-media4.fl.yelpcdn.com/assets/srv0/yelp_styleguide/c2252a4cd43e/assets/img/stars/stars_map.png" width="84"/>
                    </i>
                    <meta content="4.0" itemprop="ratingValue"/>
                   </div>
                  </div>
                  <span class="rating-qualifier">
                   <meta content="2013-05-10" itemprop="datePublished"/>
                   5/10/2013
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <div class="review_tags">
                  <span class="i-wrap ig-wrap-common i-18x18_checkin_c-common-wrap review-tag">
                   <i class="i ig-common i-18x18_checkin_c-common">
                   </i>
                   1 check-in
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <p itemprop="description" lang="en">
                  This place is extremely popular for lunch. We arrived on a weekday at 12:30pm and the place was packed.
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  What we ordered:
                  <br/>
                  Summer rolls - fresh, plump shrimp summer rolls. I really liked the peanut sauce. You order by the piece, which is actually a really great concept. That way if you want a small appetizer, you can just order however many rolls you want and you won't overeat before your entrees come.
                  <br/>
                  Vermicelli with BBQ pork and spring rolls - this is a heaping bowl of food. They're really generous with the fish sauce (thank you!). I wasn't a big fan of their BBQ pork. It's sliced really thinly and isn't the typical BBQ pork found at Vietnamese restaurants. The spring rolls, on the other hand, are delicious and perfectly crispy. The vermicelli was my favorite dish. It's fresh and light and savory all at the same time.
                  <br/>
                  Sauteed eggplant with tofu - standard dish. Good flavors. Generous with the basil.
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  Downside:
                  <br/>
                  - If you order an entree, you have to purchase rice. It's hard for me to respect asian restaurants that charge for rice when you order a carb-less main dish.
                  <br/>
                  - They have a private parking lot that maybe holds 8 cars. It's teeny tiny and it's most likely always full if you're eating during prime hours. There's street parking all along King St. Meters are only for an hour.
                 </p>

               <div class="review-wrapper">
                <div class="review-content">
                 <div class="biz-rating biz-rating-very-large clearfix">
                  <div itemprop="reviewRating" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating">
                   <div class="rating-very-large">
                    <i class="star-img stars_4" title="4.0 star rating">
                     <img alt="4.0 star rating" class="offscreen" height="303" src="//s3-media4.fl.yelpcdn.com/assets/srv0/yelp_styleguide/c2252a4cd43e/assets/img/stars/stars_map.png" width="84"/>
                    </i>
                    <meta content="4.0" itemprop="ratingValue"/>
                   </div>
                  </div>
                  <span class="rating-qualifier">
                   <meta content="2013-09-23" itemprop="datePublished"/>
                   9/23/2013
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <div class="review_tags">
                  <span class="i-wrap ig-wrap-common i-18x18_checkin_c-common-wrap review-tag">
                   <i class="i ig-common i-18x18_checkin_c-common">
                   </i>
                   1 check-in
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <p itemprop="description" lang="en">
                  First time here last weekend. I rarely come here b/c of the parking situation. They have a small but very tight lot to park in or on the street. But last Saturday after taking in a movie my friend convince me to check this place out. We were lucky and found street parking right outside of the eatery. For those of you who aren't sure where they are, they are on King street near the intersection of Pensacola on the Oceanside. So put it this way, as soon as you take a left from Pensacola to King you have to punch it to the right hand side to make sure you get near it. If you hit Piikoi you went too far.
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  Most time I start off with an appetizer of spring rolls when I hit a Vietnamese restaurant. But my friend recommended the friend garlic chicken wings. It was pretty darn ono. Nice and crispy, full of flavor and the best part was i didn't think it was that oily either. I almost wished it came in a boneless variety and then it would compete with the likes of Sugoi's or those other take out places known for their garlic chicken.
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  I'm big on Pho and since I always get the Pho Tai (beef) I can compare restaurants. My favorites so far, Pho Bistro 2 and the hole in the wall liquor store on Amana street. But this is right up there with them. Love that the onions in the broth weren't overcooked and caramelized. Lots of cilantro and green onions and the broth itself had a lot of flavor. I didn't get the sense that they put too much MSG in it which is a big plus for me since that stuff always either knocks me out or gives me a headache. 2 thumbs up, check this place out, go during an off peak time for better parking!
                 </p>
                </div>
                <div class="review-footer clearfix">

                  <div itemprop="reviewRating" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating">
                   <div class="rating-very-large">
                    <i class="star-img stars_4" title="4.0 star rating">
                     <img alt="4.0 star rating" class="offscreen" height="303" src="//s3-media4.fl.yelpcdn.com/assets/srv0/yelp_styleguide/c2252a4cd43e/assets/img/stars/stars_map.png" width="84"/>
                    </i>
                    <meta content="4.0" itemprop="ratingValue"/>
                   </div>
                  </div>
                  <span class="rating-qualifier">
                   <meta content="2013-10-21" itemprop="datePublished"/>
                   10/21/2013
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <p itemprop="description" lang="en">
                  The crab curry was good!! 4 of us had a large plate of it with French bread and a bowl of rice. We finished it so quick and I think I could have more if there's any!! We also had papaya salad, summer rolls and pho noodle. I would say pho was just okay but others were good. I'd go back there for the crab curry!!!
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  I highly recommend you to make a reservation. We had it at 5:30 so it was easy to park and we were the 1st customer but later on they kept coming and it got full house with a line outside when we leave.
                 </p>

                    <div class="action-link_icon arrange_unit">
                     <i class="i ig-common_sprite i-18x18_message_link-common_sprite align-middle">

                     Send message

                   <a class="arrange arrange--middle manage-following manage-following-add" data-csrf-token="c73d94905588e8646e5641cc887a036c840a81d37532abcbe1e7b4d95a9f9254" href="javascript:;" rel="75kabj5VFpkICIJY3ZE7ag">

               <div class="review-wrapper">
                <div class="review-content">
                 <div class="biz-rating biz-rating-very-large clearfix">
                  <div itemprop="reviewRating" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating">
                   <div class="rating-very-large">
                    <i class="star-img stars_5" title="5.0 star rating">
                     <img alt="5.0 star rating" class="offscreen" height="303" src="//s3-media4.fl.yelpcdn.com/assets/srv0/yelp_styleguide/c2252a4cd43e/assets/img/stars/stars_map.png" width="84"/>
                    </i>
                    <meta content="5.0" itemprop="ratingValue"/>
                   </div>
                  </div>
                  <span class="rating-qualifier">
                   <meta content="2014-02-05" itemprop="datePublished"/>
                   2/5/2014
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <p itemprop="description" lang="en">
                  I got a big ol' bowl of Pho.
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  One thing I hate about Pho restaurants is that they never give me that much food -- I always leave kinda unsatisfied and need to eat those leaves and bean sprouts they give you on the side to help fill my stomach. This was not the case at Bac Nam. I got one of the pho dishes (is it me or do all pho dishes taste the same). PLENTY of noodles and decent amount of meat. Ate everything and felt wonderful. These portions are how pho should always be served.
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  Bac Nam has a wide variety of food here. The menu is 4 pages. I saw curry on the menu too... and when's the last time you've heard of Vietnamese curry?? Anyway, something to try for next time.
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  Parking is limited. They only have about 8 spots in lot the back. However, if you've got a motorcycle like me, you can easily make room for yourself.
                 </p>
                </div>

               <div class="review-wrapper">
                <div class="review-content">
                 <div class="biz-rating biz-rating-very-large clearfix">
                  <div itemprop="reviewRating" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating">
                   <div class="rating-very-large">
                    <i class="star-img stars_1" title="1.0 star rating">
                     <img alt="1.0 star rating" class="offscreen" height="303" src="//s3-media4.fl.yelpcdn.com/assets/srv0/yelp_styleguide/c2252a4cd43e/assets/img/stars/stars_map.png" width="84"/>
                    </i>
                    <meta content="1.0" itemprop="ratingValue"/>
                   </div>
                  </div>
                  <span class="rating-qualifier">
                   <meta content="2014-05-04" itemprop="datePublished"/>
                   5/4/2014
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <p itemprop="description" lang="en">
                  Very disappointed. I decided to give this place a try because of some good reviews. Very sad.
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  When I first came in, the guy who I think was the owner was initially nice. We waited 10 minutes to be seated on a Saturday night. We ordered the pho with beef balls, chicken curry and spring rolls.
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  Spring rolls: Decent taste. The skin had a dark color which I think was either old spring rolls or old oil.
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  Pho: Ok tasting. Hands started swelling, possibly because of msg.
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  Chicken curry: WORST. ALL BONES! The guy told me that's how traditional Vietnamese curry is. I can understand that they are trying to be authentic but if 90% of my chicken is bones, that's just horrible. I asked if I could trade it for the beef and all he said was "what about your chicken curry?" If you like sucking on bones for $11 with chewy bread (extra $1.75), eat this.
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  Overall very disappointed...
                 </p>

               <div class="review-wrapper">
                <div class="review-content">
                 <div class="biz-rating biz-rating-very-large clearfix">
                  <div itemprop="reviewRating" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating">
                   <div class="rating-very-large">
                    <i class="star-img stars_5" title="5.0 star rating">
                     <img alt="5.0 star rating" class="offscreen" height="303" src="//s3-media4.fl.yelpcdn.com/assets/srv0/yelp_styleguide/c2252a4cd43e/assets/img/stars/stars_map.png" width="84"/>
                    </i>
                    <meta content="5.0" itemprop="ratingValue"/>
                   </div>
                  </div>
                  <span class="rating-qualifier">
                   <meta content="2013-03-18" itemprop="datePublished"/>
                   3/18/2013
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <p itemprop="description" lang="en">
                  Pho-natic [fuh-nat-ik]: n. a person with an extreme and uncritical enthusiasm for pho.
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  Signs and Symptoms:
                  <br/>
                  1. Conditioned to salivate at a morsel of tender, rare steak.
                  <br/>
                  2. Sauce hijacker
                  <br/>
                  3. Garnish hoarder
                  <br/>
                  4. Makes excuses to eat pho when sick, cold, tired, or breathing.
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  I blame my phonaticism on Renee L. who introduced me to pho on a rainy Wednesday in March of 2011. One bite. Just one tidbit of that fish sauce and chili garlic paste short circuited the taste center of my brain.
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  There are a myriad of pho restaurants on the island. Pho Bistro 2, Pho One, and Super Pho serve way decent, traditional pho IMO. However, it really depends on personal preference. Are you a meat person? A sauce lover? A broth fiend?
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  No matter what category you designate yourself as, nothing compares to the "Pho Real" Granddaddy: Bac Nam.
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  Tam, the patriarch of the business, is one friendly Vietnamese owner. He will smile, muttering jokes when taking your order with light hearted, colloquial conversation. Ask about his teenage daughter who can be seen serving tables and he'll roll his eyes in endearing fatherly fashion and quip, "It's soo much easier with boys. You don't have to worry about them!" Meanwhile, his wife prepares the dishes for both locals and tourists who pack their tiny restaurant. And it's PACKED with Japanese tourists who obviously hear marvelous things about the restaurant to trek into the Pensacola/King district.
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  For me, it's all in the rich broth. The sauces, garnish, and meat do add to the flavor but the broth is beyond compare. And even if you're not a phonatic, read the other reviews for equally scrumptious bites.
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  Curries. Stews. Soups...what's not to love. I savor their garlic ung choi and summer rolls. Bac Nam holds a nice balance of reasonable prices for food cooked as if you were sitting with Tam and his family in their dining room. I'd love to be a fly on that wall...
                 </p>
                </div>
                <div class="review-footer clearfix">

                 <p itemprop="description" lang="en">
                  Bac Nam is by far my favorite vietnamese restaurant! I came there so often I didn't even have to order anymore they just brought me my usual. So much flavor, excellent service... I'm so mad I had to move off the island now I have to find a new favorite in Texas. But anytime I'm in Hawaii please believe I'm running there for my shrimp spring rolls!

                   <div class="rating-very-large">
                    <i class="star-img stars_1" title="1.0 star rating">
                     <img alt="1.0 star rating" class="offscreen" height="303" src="//s3-media4.fl.yelpcdn.com/assets/srv0/yelp_styleguide/c2252a4cd43e/assets/img/stars/stars_map.png" width="84"/>
                    </i>
                    <meta content="1.0" itemprop="ratingValue"/>
                   </div>
                  </div>
                  <span class="rating-qualifier">
                   <meta content="2014-10-07" itemprop="datePublished"/>
                   10/7/2014
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <p itemprop="description" lang="en">
                  I'm really not sure why this place got such good reviews, but this place DOES NOT deserve that high of a rating. I ordered the beef curry, spring rolls, and lemongrass chicken plate. The beef curry was a huge disappointment. The curry tasted like water, there was zero flavor and it just tasted like nothing. Possibly the worst dish I've ever eaten. The lemongrass chicken was better, but the meat was on the tougher side and lacked sufficient amounts of pungent lemongrass. The spring rolls were delicious, but seriously how hard is it to.make spring rolls? Never going back here ever again!
                 </p>
                </div>
                <div class="review-footer clearfix">
                 <div class="rateReview voting-feedback" data-review-id="ilVHHwUqvXVNjnc0zG9SvQ">
